                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_dinar_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    multiply = scope:player_dinar_to_gold.money_value_rapported_inflation
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                    add = var:stockpiling_dinar_state_1_selle_in_gold
                }

                #########
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_dinar_state_1
                    subtract = owner.stockpiling_dinar_state_sell_vriablity
                }
            }
        }
        scope:player_dinar_to_gold = {
            every_scope_state = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        subtract = scope:gold_to_dinar_seller_capital_state.var:stockpiling_dinar_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_dinar_state_1
                        add = scope:gold_to_dinar_seller.stockpiling_dinar_state_sell_vriablity
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = stockpiling_dinar_state_sell_vriablity_for_toast
                value =  scope:gold_to_dinar_seller.stockpiling_dinar_state_sell_vriablity
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    stockpiling_dinar_state_sell_vriablity > 1
                }
                post_notification = your_currency_dinar_are_sell_message
                #post_notification = your_currency_dinar_are_sell_toast
            }
        }
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                set_variable = {
                	name = stockpiling_dinar_state_1_selle_in_gold
                	value = 0
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

#krone
ai_buy_player_currency_1_krone = {

    every_country = {
        limit  = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        save_scope_as = player_krone_to_gold
    }

    root = {
        save_scope_as = gold_to_krone_seller
    }

    scope:gold_to_krone_seller = {
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                save_scope_as = gold_to_krone_seller_capital_state

                change_variable = {
                    name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                    subtract = stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold_scripted_for_player
                }

                #########
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_krone_state_1
                    add = owner.stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity
                }
            }
        }
        scope:player_krone_to_gold = {
            every_scope_state = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    set_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        value =  scope:gold_to_krone_seller.stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        multiply = owner.money_value_rapported_inflation
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        add = var:stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold
                    }

                    #########
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_krone_state_1
                        subtract = scope:gold_to_krone_seller.stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity
                    }

                    #########
                    #Reset
                    set_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        value = 0
                    }
                }
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity > 1
                }
                set_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity_for_toast
                    value =  scope:gold_to_krone_seller.stockpiling_krone_state_buy_vriablity
                }
                post_notification = your_currency_krone_are_buy_message
            }
        }
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                set_variable = {
                	name = stockpiling_krone_state_1_buy_in_gold
                	value = 0
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    set_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        value =  scope:gold_to_qiran_seller.stockpiling_qiran_state_buy_vriablity
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        multiply = owner.money_value_rapported_inflation
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        add = var:stockpiling_qiran_state_1_buy_in_gold
                    }

                    #########
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1
                        subtract = scope:gold_to_qiran_seller.stockpiling_qiran_state_buy_vriablity
                    }

                    #########
                    #Reset
                    set_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_buy_in_gold
                        value = 0
                    }
                }
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    stockpiling_qiran_state_buy_vriablity > 1
                }
                set_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_qiran_state_buy_vriablity_for_toast
                    value =  scope:gold_to_qiran_seller.stockpiling_qiran_state_buy_vriablity
                }
                post_notification = your_currency_qiran_are_buy_message
            }
        }
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                set_variable = {
                	name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_buy_in_gold
                	value = 0
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
ai_sell_player_currency_1_qiran = {

    every_country = {
        limit  = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        save_scope_as = player_qiran_to_gold
    }

    root = {
        save_scope_as = gold_to_qiran_seller
    }


    scope:gold_to_qiran_seller = {
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                save_scope_as = gold_to_qiran_seller_capital_state

                set_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    value = owner.stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    multiply = scope:player_qiran_to_gold.money_value_rapported_inflation
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                    add = var:stockpiling_qiran_state_1_selle_in_gold
                }

                #########
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1
                    subtract = owner.stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity
                }
            }
        }
        scope:player_qiran_to_gold = {
            every_scope_state = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        subtract = scope:gold_to_qiran_seller_capital_state.var:stockpiling_qiran_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1
                        add = scope:gold_to_qiran_seller.stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity
                    }
                }
            }
            set_variable = {
                name = stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity_for_toast
                value =  scope:gold_to_qiran_seller.stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    stockpiling_qiran_state_sell_vriablity > 1
                }
                post_notification = your_currency_qiran_are_sell_message
                #post_notification = your_currency_qiran_are_sell_toast
            }
        }
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                set_variable = {
                	name = stockpiling_qiran_state_1_selle_in_gold
                	value = 0
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

########################################################
#experimental

ai_buy_unbalance_currency = {
    every_country = {
        limit  = {
            money_supply > money_supply_stockpile_by_other_country
            money_supply > 100000000
            has_modifier = has_central_bank
            not = {
                or = {
                    is_subject_of = root
                    is_subject_type = subject_type_customs_union
                    is_subject_type = subject_type_protectorate
                }
            }
        }
        save_scope_as = seller_of_unbalance_currency
    }

    root = {
        save_scope_as = buyer_of_unbalance_currency
    }

    #########

    set_variable  = {
        name = unbalance_currency_money_value
        value = scope:seller_of_unbalance_currency.money_value_rapported_inflation
    }
    set_variable  = {
        name = unbalance_currency_quantity
        value = 10000000 #10M
    }
    set_variable  = {
        name = unbalance_currency_in_gold_1
        value = var:unbalance_currency_money_value
    }
    set_variable  = {
        name = unbalance_currency_in_gold_2
        multiplier = var:unbalance_currency_quantity
    }

    #########

    scope:buyer_of_unbalance_currency = {
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                save_scope_as = buyer_of_unbalance_currency_capital_state

                change_variable = {
                    name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                    subtract = var:unbalance_currency_in_gold_2
                }

                #########

                #all currency

                if = {
                    limit = {
                        scope:seller_of_unbalance_currency.seller_of_unbalance_currency_has_law_rouble = 1
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_rouble_state_1
                        add = owner.var:unbalance_currency_quantity
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        scope:seller_of_unbalance_currency = {
            every_scope_state = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        add = scope:buyer_of_unbalance_currency.var:unbalance_currency_in_gold_2
                    }

                    #########

                    #all currency

                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            seller_of_unbalance_currency_has_law_rouble = 1
                        }
                        change_variable = {
                            name = stockpiling_rouble_state_1
                            subtract = 10000000 #scope:buyer_of_unbalance_currency.var:unbalance_currency_quantity
                        }
                    }



                    #########
                    #Reset
                    #set_variable = {
                    #    name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1_buy_in_gold
                    #    value = 0
                    #}
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
ai_sell_currency_on_currency_balance = {

    every_country = {
        limit  = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        save_scope_as = is_player_for_notification
    }

    every_country = {
        limit  = {
            has_modifier = global_monetary_reference
            has_law = law_type:law_sterling_currency
        }
        save_scope_as = global_monetary_reference_sterling_to_gold
    }

    root = {
        save_scope_as = gold_to_sterling_seller
    }

    scope:gold_to_sterling_seller = {
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                save_scope_as = gold_to_sterling_seller_capital_state

                set_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    value = owner.stockpiling_sterling_state_sell_vriablity
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    multiply = scope:global_monetary_reference_sterling_to_gold.money_value_rapported_inflation
                }
                change_variable = {
                    name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                    add = var:stockpiling_sterling_state_1_selle_in_gold
                }

                #########
                change_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1
                    subtract = owner.stockpiling_sterling_state_sell_vriablity
                }
            }
        }
        scope:global_monetary_reference_sterling_to_gold = {
            every_scope_state = {
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                        is_capital = yes
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = central_bank_gold_reserves_state_1
                        subtract = scope:gold_to_sterling_seller_capital_state.var:stockpiling_sterling_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    }
                    change_variable = {
                        name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1
                        add = scope:gold_to_sterling_seller.stockpiling_sterling_state_sell_vriablity
                    }
                }
            }

            set_variable = {
                name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1_sell_in_gold_for_toast
                value =  scope:gold_to_sterling_seller.stockpiling_sterling_state_sell_vriablity
            }

            if = {
                limit = {
                    stockpiling_sterling_state_sell_vriablity > 1
                }

                post_notification = global_monetary_reference_are_sterling_sell_message
                scope:is_player_for_notification = {
                    post_notification = global_monetary_reference_are_sterling_sell_message
                }
            }
        }
        every_scope_state = {
            if = {
                limit = {
                    has_modifier = bank_central_historic_place
                    is_capital = yes
                }
                set_variable = {
                    name = stockpiling_sterling_state_1_selle_in_gold
                    value = 0
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
